  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{

  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

ghost function Sum(s: seq<int>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0 else Sum(s[..|s|-1]) + s[|s|-1]
}

// Occupancy after processing all stops described by a and b:
// total who boarded minus total who exited
ghost function Occupancy(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
{
  Sum(b) - Sum(a)
}

// A capacity is valid if it is non-negative and never exceeded
// at any stop (after the first k stops, for every k from 1 to n)
ghost predicate IsValidCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

// The minimum capacity: valid, and no smaller value is valid
ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {

    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}
```

// Occupancy after processing all stops described by a and b:

{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{

    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

    assert Sum([x]) == x;
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
    assert Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + Sum([x]);
    assert Sum([x]) == x;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

  if |s| == 0 then 0 else Sum(s[..|s|-1]) + s[|s|-1]
}

// Occupancy after processing all stops described by a and b:
// total who boarded minus total who exited
ghost function Occupancy(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
{
  Sum(b) - Sum(a)
}

// A capacity is valid if it is non-negative and never exceeded
// at any stop (after the first k stops, for every k from 1 to n)
ghost predicate IsValidCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

// The minimum capacity: valid, and no smaller value is valid
ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c

  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{

    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

// at any stop (after the first k stops, for every k from 1 to n)
ghost predicate IsValidCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

// The minimum capacity: valid, and no smaller value is valid
ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {

  }

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{

  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0

    // Update capacity if needed

      capacity := current;

    i := i + 1;

{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

{

    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c

  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

{

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    // When s is empty, s + [x] is just [x]
    assert Sum(s + [x]) == Sum([x]) ;
    assert Sum([x]) == x ;
    assert Sum(s) == 0 ;
    assert Sum(s) + x == x ;
    assert Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x ;
  } else {
    // When s is non-empty, the last element of s + [x] is x
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s ;
    assert Sum((s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1]) == Sum(s) ;
    assert Sum(s + [x]) == Sum((s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1]) + (s + [x])[|s + [x]| - 1] ;
    assert (s + [x])[|s + [x]| - 1] == x ;
    assert Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x ;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {

    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }

  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

// The minimum capacity: valid, and no smaller value is valid
ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

ghost function Sum(s: seq<int>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0 else Sum(s[..|s|-1]) + s[|s|-1]
}

ghost function Occupancy(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
{
  Sum(b) - Sum(a)
}

ghost predicate IsValidCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|

  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
    assert Sum([x]) == Sum([]) + x;
    assert Sum([x]) == 0 + x;
    assert Sum([x]) == x;
    assert Sum([]) + x == x;
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
    assert Sum(s + [x]) == Sum((s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1]) + (s + [x])[|s + [x]| - 1];
    assert Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + (s + [x])[|s + [x]| - 1];
    assert (s + [x])[|s + [x]| - 1] == x;
    assert Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

```dafny
ghost function Sum(s: seq<int>): int
  decreases |s|
{
  if |s| == 0 then 0 else Sum(s[..|s|-1]) + s[|s|-1]
}

// Occupancy after processing all stops described by a and b:
// total who boarded minus total who exited
ghost function Occupancy(a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>): int
  requires |a| == |b|
{
  Sum(b) - Sum(a)
}

// A capacity is valid if it is non-negative and never exceeded
// at any stop (after the first k stops, for every k from 1 to n)
ghost predicate IsValidCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  c >= 0 &&
  forall k | 1 <= k <= n :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= c
}

// The minimum capacity: valid, and no smaller value is valid
ghost predicate IsMinimumCapacity(c: int, n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {
    assert (s + [x])[..|s + [x]| - 1] == s;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0

lemma SumAppend(s: seq<int>, x: int)
  ensures Sum(s + [x]) == Sum(s) + x
{
  if |s| == 0 {
    assert s + [x] == [x];
  } else {

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
{
  IsValidCapacity(c, n, a, b) &&
  forall c' | 0 <= c' < c :: !IsValidCapacity(c', n, a, b)
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - b[i] + a[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}

method Tram(n: int, a: seq<int>, b: seq<int>) returns (capacity: int)
  requires 0 <= n <= |a| && n <= |b|
  ensures IsMinimumCapacity(capacity, n, a, b)
{
  var current := 0;
  capacity := 0;
  var i := 0;
  while i < n
    invariant 0 <= i <= n
    invariant current == Occupancy(a[..i], b[..i])
    invariant capacity >= 0
    invariant forall k | 1 <= k <= i :: Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k]) <= capacity
    invariant capacity == 0 || exists k | 1 <= k <= i :: capacity == Occupancy(a[..k], b[..k])
  {
    SumAppend(a[..i], a[i]);
    SumAppend(b[..i], b[i]);
    current := current - a[i] + b[i];
    if current > capacity {
      capacity := current;
    }
    i := i + 1;
  }
}
